NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

811

I, G. Murali was born at Chennai, Tamil Nadu as a male child to Mr. N. Ganesan on 28th March 1977 and
residing at No. 5, Bajanai Koil Street, Kodambakkam, Chennai-600 024, and now for the past five years residing at
No. 33, Sivanandam Street, Near Vidya Thetre, West Tambaram, Chennai-600 045. After an Elborate Sexual
Reassignment Suregery she has been living as a female (reference Dr. V. Jayaraman MS, MCH, MNAMS, DIP. N.B., PHD,
FICS) Clinical surgery, Kilpauk Medical College and Hospital Chennai-600 010. Then through clinical examination under
Dr. V. Jayaraman MS, MCH, MNAMS, DIP, N.B. PHD, FICS shows that I could be treated as a female G. Murali shall
henceforth be known as G. GRACE.
Chennai,

G. MURALI.

28th March 2013.
